			give_nickname = nick_the_hairy
			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		}

	10867.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			# We can guess that he didn't get on well with his cousin, as he sided against him in later conflicts.
			set_relation_rival = { target = character:barcelona_00003 reason = rival_historical }
			# And his possible-surrogate father (or else uhh... bitter rival) got on well with the neighbouring Banu Qasi.
			set_relation_potential_friend = character:73813
			# Will eventually become something of a local folk hero, so is clearly quite popular. We give him a little political capital to spend already.
			add_prestige_experience = 500
			add_prestige = 500
			# Finally, make him friends with his brother so that he's less likely to be immediately murdered by his cousin.
			set_relation_friend = { reason = friend_generic_history target = character:73996 }
		}
	}
	10875.6.27 = {
		add_spouse = 70151 # Guinidilda
	}
	10897.8.11 = {
